/*Table structure for table `deletehash` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `deletehash`;

CREATE TABLE `deletehash` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `hash` char(8) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `hash` (`hash`),
  KEY `uid` (`uid`),
  CONSTRAINT `DeleteHash_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=750 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `garbagedmembers` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `garbagedmembers`;

CREATE TABLE `garbagedmembers` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `username` varchar(30) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `password` char(128) NOT NULL,
  `salt` char(64) NOT NULL,
  `auto` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=295 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `keyaccess` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `keyaccess`;

CREATE TABLE `keyaccess` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `page` char(6) NOT NULL,
  `username` char(30) NOT NULL,
  `key` char(20) NOT NULL,
  `expiration` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `key` (`key`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uid` (`uid`,`page`,`username`),
  CONSTRAINT `KeyAccess_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=9 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `loginattempts` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `loginattempts`;

CREATE TABLE `loginattempts` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  KEY `uid` (`uid`),
  CONSTRAINT `LoginAttempts_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Data for the table `loginattempts` */

/*Table structure for table `mailreset` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `mailreset`;

CREATE TABLE `mailreset` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `new_email` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `verified` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `hash` char(128) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`uid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  UNIQUE KEY `new_email` (`new_email`),
  CONSTRAINT `MailReset_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Data for the table `mailreset` */

/*Table structure for table `mailresetattempts` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `mailresetattempts`;

CREATE TABLE `mailresetattempts` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  KEY `uid` (`uid`),
  CONSTRAINT `MailResetAttempts_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Data for the table `mailresetattempts` */

/*Table structure for table `mailsentattempts` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `mailsentattempts`;

CREATE TABLE `mailsentattempts` (
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  CONSTRAINT `MailSentAttempts_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`email`) REFERENCES `members` (`email`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Data for the table `mailsentattempts` */

/*Table structure for table `members` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `members`;

CREATE TABLE `members` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `username` varchar(30) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `verified` int DEFAULT '0',
  `password` char(128) NOT NULL,
  `salt` char(64) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `username` (`username`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=10151 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `passwordchangeattempts` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `passwordchangeattempts`;

CREATE TABLE `passwordchangeattempts` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  KEY `uid` (`uid`),
  CONSTRAINT `PasswordChangeAttempts_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `passwordreset` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `passwordreset`;

CREATE TABLE `passwordreset` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `hash` char(128) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`uid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  CONSTRAINT `PasswordReset_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Data for the table `passwordreset` */

/*Table structure for table `usersettings` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `usersettings`;

CREATE TABLE `usersettings` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `setting` char(32) NOT NULL,
  `string` char(64) DEFAULT NULL,
  `boolean` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`uid`,`setting`),
  CONSTRAINT `UserSettings_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `valuationgroups` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `valuationgroups`;

CREATE TABLE `valuationgroups` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` char(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=39 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

/*Table structure for table `verification` */

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `verification`;

CREATE TABLE `verification` (
  `uid` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `hash` char(128) NOT NULL,
  `datetime` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`uid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  CONSTRAINT `Verification_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`uid`) REFERENCES `members` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;
